Breeze B-Library
metadata O
is O
information O
about O
all O
the O
objects O
you O
have O
to O
work O
with O
. O

You O
can O
fetch O
metadata O
from O
server-side O
or O
you O
can O
create O
metadata O
by O
yourself O
and O
work O
with O
it O
. O

If O
you O
want O
to O
work O
with O
your O
server-side O
objects O
in O
breeze B-Library
you O
create O
an O
entity O
manager O
with O
var O
entityManager O
= O
new O
breeze.EntityManager('api/Db') O
; O
where O
api/db O
is O
your O
asp.net B-Library
controller O
. O

This O
controller O
should O
have O
a O
Metadata() O
method O
which O
returns O
repository.Metadata() O
. O

In O
js B-Programming_Language
you O
call O
entityManager.fetchMetadata() O
.then(success,failed) O
; O
After O
the O
promise O
of O
fetchMetadata() O
is O
resolved O
, O
breeze B-Library
metadata O
of O
variable O
entityManager O
is O
full-filled O
and O
you O
can O
start O
working O
with O
your O
server-side B-Application
objects O
in O
js B-Programming_Language
with O
breeze B-Library
! O

But O
you O
can O
also O
work O
without O
any O
metadata O
from O
server-side B-Application
and O
create O
it O
on O
the O
fly O
in O
your O
js B-Programming_Language
code O
. O

You O
create O
your O
own O
metadataStore B-Library_Class
, O
attach O
it O
to O
entitymanager B-Library_Class
. O

Pseudo O
code O
: O

CODE_BLOCK O
: O
A_3236 O
( O
code O
omitted O
for O
annotation O
) O

Here O
is O
a O
working O
sample O
from O
breeze B-Library
with O
on-the-fly O
metadata O
http://www.breezejs.com/breeze-labs/breezedirectivesvalidation O

You O
click O
on O
code O
button B-User_Interface_Element
or O
just O
go O
to O
http://plnkr.co/edit/lxPAbIJmRaLmyagXQAFC?p=info O
to O
see O
sources O

Also O
take O
a O
look O
at O
this O
link O
in O

Yes O
, O
it O
is O
wise O
to O
use O
multiple O
ports B-Device
when O
doing O

transfers O
. O

It O
would O

to O

and O

( O

still O

transfers O
) O
. O

But O
I O

not O

to O
use O
three O
fixed O
ports B-Device
. O

Use O
one O
port B-Device
for O
all O

and O

arbitrary O

for O

. O

: O

in O

. O

. O

Then O

.NET B-Library

( O

Windows B-Operating_System
will O
overwrite O
the O
boot O
sector O
whenever O
you O
install O
it O
. O

In O
general O
install O
windows B-Operating_System
first O
then O
linux B-Operating_System
. O

You O
can O
repair O
the O
grub B-Application
by O
booting O
from O
a O
live O
disk B-Device
of O
linux B-Operating_System
Mint O
and O
there O
should O
be O
an O
option O
to O
repair-boot O
, O
which O
will O
repair O
your O
grub B-Application
. O

Restart O
it O
and O
now O
you O
should O
be O
able O
to O
see O
both O
the O
OS O
. O

Or O
you O
can O
boot O
from O
a O
live O
cd B-Device
and O
perform O
the O
following O
steps O
: O

Boot O
from O
a O
live O
CD B-Device
( O
CD/DVD B-Device
or O
flash B-Device
drive I-Device
) O
. O

Become O
root O
or O
use O
sudo O
with O
commands O
below O
. O

List O
the O
available O
partitions O
if O
needed O
: O
fdisk O
-l O

Windows B-Operating_System
will O
almost O
certainly O
exist O
on O
/dev/sda1 O
: O
mount O
/dev/sda1 O
/mnt O

Reinstall O
GRUB B-Application
in O
the O
MBR B-Device
: O
grub-install O
--root-directory O
= O
/mnt/ O
/dev/sda O

Reboot O
: O
shutdown O
-r O
now O

Restore O
the O
GRUB B-Application
menu O
: O
update-grub O

Thanks O
to O
@christopher O
for O
the O
above O
answer O
. O

The O
DevTools B-Application
can O

any O

that O

, O

that O

A O
node B-Application
app O
will O
stay O
alive O
as O
long O
as O
there O
are O
active O
elements O
that O
can O
still O
receive O
events O
. O

This O
can O
include O
a O
TCP O
connection O
, O
a O
listening O
server B-Application
, O
a O
timer O
, O
etc O
.. O
. O

As O
soon O
as O
none O
of O
those O
exist O
any O
more O
and O
the O
event O
queue B-Data_Structure
is O
empty O
and O

flow O
of O
control O
returns O
back O
to O
the O
system O
( O
e.g O
. O
no O
JS B-Programming_Language
is O
executing O
) O
, O
then O
the O
node B-Application
app O
will O
shut O
itself O
down O
. O

The O
idea O
is O
that O
if O
nothing O
is O
running O
that O
could O
possible O
create O
more O
events O
in O
the O
future O
, O

can O

in O
this O
node B-Application
app O

be O
done O
. O

saying O
that O
when O

to O

, O

wo O

start O

, O

issue O
. O

need O
to O
do O
some O

of O
errors O
and O

to O

why O

As O
a O
verbal O
procedure O
, O
you O
can O
do O
: O

Allocate O
an O
array B-Data_Structure
of O
pointers B-Data_Type
to O
chars B-Data_Type

Read O
all O
lines O
of O
the O
file O
. O

Allocate O
a O
new O
string B-Data_Type
for O
each O
line O
and O
put O
in O
the O
array B-Data_Structure

If O
the O
array B-Data_Structure
is O
too O
small O
, O
then O
use O
realloc O
to O
make O
it O
larger O
. O

Read O
about O
realloc O
to O
avoid O
common O
errors O
. O

Once O
the O
file O
has O
been O
read O
, O
use O
your O
own O
bubble O
sort O
or O
the O
library O
's O

to O
sort O
the O
array B-Data_Structure
. O

Read O
about O
qsort O
. O

Once O
sorted O
, O
re-write O
file3 O
from O
the O
array B-Data_Structure
. O

Coding O
this O
is O
a O
nice O
excercise O
that O
I O
leave O
to O
you O
. O

See O

If O

When O
you O
use O
Chrome B-Application
and O
request O
the O
same O
resource O
in O
multiple O
tabs B-User_Interface_Element
, O
it O
will O
wait O
for O
the O
resource O
to O
finish O
downloading O
in O
one O
. O

The O
reason O
is O
that O
if O
the O
headers O
allow O
, O
the O
second O
tab B-User_Interface_Element
will O
load O
from O
cache O
, O
rather O
than O
reloading O
it O
from O
the O
server B-Application
. O

This O
has O
nothing O
to O
do O
with O
your O
server B-Application
configuration O
, O
but O
more O
to O
do O
with O
your O
flawed O
test O
method O
. O

Fire O
off O
a O
couple O
wget O
calls O
from O
the O
command B-Application
line I-Application
, O
and O
this O
will O
likely O
work O
as O
expected O
. O

You O
can O
also O
verify O
that O
this O
is O
happening O
by O
using O

debugging O
proxy O
, O
such O
as O

, O
or O

software O
, O

as O

. O

You O

more O

. O

Upon O

The O

partitions O

usually O
written O
in O

board O
's O

file O
. O

You O
can O
override O
that O
by O
passing O
the O
kernel B-Application
a O
mtdparts O
option O
. O

More O
info O
here O
. O

Also O
mtdinfo O
and O
/proc/mtd O
describe O
the O
start-end O
of O
each O
partition O
and O
its O
name O
. O

: O

An O
example O
of O
the O

partition O
table B-Data_Structure

in O

( O

omitted O
for O
annotation O
) O

} O

5 O

. O

perhaps O
you O
should O

to O

= O
sm_11 O

sm B-Device

which O
supported O

operations O
on O
global O
memory O
while O
your O
GPU B-Device
supports O
SM B-Device
2.0 O
. O

Hence O
there O
is O
no O
reason O
to O
compile O
for O
SM B-Device
1.1 O
unless O
for O
backward O
compatibility O
. O

One O
possible O
issue O
could O
be O
that O
SM B-Device
1.1 O
does O
not O
support O
atomic B-Application
operations O
on O
64-bit O
ints B-Data_Type
in O
global O
memory O
. O

So O
I O
would O
suggest O
you O
recompile O
the O
code O
without O
-arch O
option O

or O
use O
-arch O
= O
sm_20 O
if O
you O
like O
